9th-32nd Decklists
==================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on September 3, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/hosler.jpg)
By Corbin Hosler











The Top 8 decks get all the attention, but the real story of the tournament can be found by going a little deeper. Which is why we’ve compiled the Top 32 decklists from Grand Prix Washington D.C. for a glimpse into the decks that fell just outside the Top 8.







#### Julian Leal's Ramunap Red, Grand Prix Washington D.C., 9th place


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
